CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));
